		featureGroupIndicators: 7fcffefe [bit length 32, 0111 1111  1100 1111  1111 1110  1111 1110 decimal value 2144337662]
			0... .... = Indicator 1: Intra-subframe freq hopping for PUSCH scheduled by UL grant; DCI format 3a; Aperiodic CQI/PMI/RI report on PUSCH: Mode 2-0 & 2-2 - Not supported
			.1.. .... = Indicator 2: Simultaneous CQI & ACK/NACK on PUCCH (format 2a/2b); Absolute TPC command for PUSCH; Resource alloc type 1 for PDSCH; Periodic CQI/PMI/RI report on PUCCH: Mode 2-0 & 2-1 - Supported
			..1. .... = Indicator 3: 5bit RLC UM SN; 7bit PDCP SN - Supported
			...1 .... = Indicator 4: Short DRX cycle - Supported
